 Here the talk of the last five T20 World Cup matches, which once caught everyone's breath, and which will always be remembered by cricket fans
 1) bharat banaam pakistan (group match), 2007pehle tii20 vishwa cap main bharat-pakistan ke bich hua group match kise yaad nahin hoga
 It would not be wrong if it is called the most exciting match ever
 match kaa faisla ball out se hua
 Both teams scored 141 runs in the scheduled overs and the match was tied
 aakhri over main pakistan ko jeetne ke liye 12 ranon kii jarurat thi or uske paas 4 wicket baaki the
 While the last two balls required 1 run, Misbah could not score a single and was run out on the last ball
 baad main ball out se faisla bharat ke paksh main gaya
 2) India vs Pakistan (final match), 2007 The same World Cup final also saw both teams face to face, and the match dice on every ball
 kabhi bharat to kabhi pakistan ke paksh main match jhukaa
 It was difficult to predict the winner until the last over
 donon deshon ke logon kii saansen ruk si gayi thim
 a wrong shot from Misbah in the last over of Joginder Sharma snatched the match from Pakistan and put India in the bag
 pakistan ko aakhri over main 13 ranon kii aavashyaktaa thi, or uske paas sirf ek wicket tha
 After scoring seven runs off the first two balls, Misbah hit the back of the wicket on Joginder's fourth ball, which was caught by Sreesanth and the first World Cup was named for Team India
 3) australia banaam zimbabwe, 2007world tii20 pehali baar 2007 main khelaa gaya or is pehle hi sanskaran main zimbabwe kii team ne dikhaa diya ki wo ulatpher karne main kitni maahir he
 The Australian team, which had won the 50-over World Cup five times, fell victim to this format
 2007 world cap ke lig match main is team ko apane se behad kamjor zimbabwe se haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa
 This result shocked everyone
 pehle khelte hue australia ne maatr 138 ran banaae
 The Zimbabwean team achieved this goal with just one ball remaining and also made the biggest upset of the T20 World Cup
 4) england banaam netherland, 2009duusare world cap kaa pehla hi match hi behad romaanchak rahaa
 Playing the weakened Netherlands, this match of England reached the last ball
 162 ranon kaa peechha karne utari netherland ko aakhri over main 7 ranon kii aavashkata thi
 In this over, Broad left a catch on his own and then England's fielders also missed two run outs
 nateeja ye rahaa ki netherland ne aakhri over kii aakhri gend par match apane naam kar liya
 5) South Africa vs New Zealand, in another close match of the 20092009 World Cup, New Zealand lost by just one run
 maatr 129 ranon kaa peechha karne utari kiwi team 5 wicket haath main hone ke baavjood bhi 20 overon main sirf 127 hi bana saki
 For the Kiwi team, this defeat was also a never forgettable defeat
 6) australia banaam pakistan, 20102010 ke world cap main australia or pakistan ke bich hue duusare semifinal match main romaanchakta kii har had paar hui
 Australia, who were almost on the verge of defeat, won this match in such a way that no one was confident
 ek samay australia ko jeet ke liye 18 gendon main 48 ran chahie the, or sirf teen wicket haath main the
 At this time, Mr
 Cricket Mike Hussey played an innings of 60 runs in just 24 balls and with one ball remaining, the team reached the target of 192 runs
 australia ko aakhri over main jeet ke liye 18 ran chahie the
 Hussey took 22 runs in this over of Saeed Ajmal to lead his team to the final
 7) westeindies banaam newjiland, 20122012 world cap ke group match main westeindies auranujilandke bich muqabla super over tak ja pahunchaa
 Despite the low scoring, the match was very exciting

 ' Some of the last poignant images of Girish Karnad are made of resistance meetings where he was seen arriving at the 'main Bhi Urban Naxal' and 'not in My Name'

 But the real value of Girish Karnad is much bigger than these resistance meetings
 unke naatakon main bhartiya chetana kii prashnakulata apane shikhar par dikhaai padati he
 Using the tools of myth and history, he encounters contemporary reality and very poignantly points at socio-political irony
 'hayvadan' jaisi jatil katha or sanrachana vaala naatak hindi yaa bhartiya bhashaaon main hi nahin, duniya ke rangamanch main durlabh he
 In this play he points to multiple duality simultaneously - the duality of mind and body, the duality of humanity and animalism, the duality of love and devotion and ultimately the duality of man's relationship with God
 isi tarah 'tughlaq' main vah udaartaa or sanak ke bich jhulate ek mahatvakankshi shaasha ke bahaane satta or janata ke rishton, darbari samskruti kii patanshiltaa or ek banate-bikharate desh kii traasadee ko kai konon se dekhte hai

 aisi hi kahani he baliya ke rahane vaale primary teacher saurabh singh kii
 Saurabh has been ranked eighth in the recently announced Uttar Pradesh PCS 2016 results
 saurabh ke naanaa kaa sapana tha ki unka naati adhyaaapak na banakar rah jaae balki kuch bada mukaam hasil kare
 Even today, Saurabh has not forgotten the things told by his maternal grandfather
